   h,m=map(int,s.split(':')); return h*60+m\n\ndef binom_sf(k,n,p):\n    return sum(comb(n,i)*(p**i)*((1-p)**(n-i)) for i in range(k,n+1))\nwo=pd.read_csv('/app/maintenance_work_orders.csv')\nrows=[]\nfor rp in wo['report_path']:\n    d={}\n    for line in Path('/app', rp).read_text().splitlines():\n        if ': ' in ORDER'],'machine_id':d['MACHINE'],'technician_id':d['TECHNICIAN'],'maint_day':int(d['DAY']),'completed_min':t(d['COMPLETED'])})\nsvc=pd.DataFrame(rows)\nsvc['maint_abs']=svc['maint_day']*1440+svc['completed_min']\nsvc=svc.sort_values(['machine_id','maint_abs','work_order_id']).reset_index(drop=True)\nsvc['window_idx']=svc.groupby('machine_id').cumcount()\n\nb=pd.read_csv('/app/production_batches.csv').merge(pd.read_csv('/app/machine_assignment_log.csv')[['day','job_id','machine_id','start_time']], right_on=['day','job_id','machine_id'])\nb['start_min']=b['start_time'].map(t)\nb['start_abs']=b['production_day']*1440+b['start_min']\nins=pd.read_csv('/app/quality_inspections.csv')[['batch_id','inspection_result','rejected_pct']]\nb=b.merge(ins, m=svc[svc.machine_id==machine_id].sort_values(['maint_abs','work_order_id'])\n    parts.append(pd.merge_asof(g.sort_values(['start_abs','batch_id']),m,left_on='start_abs',right_on='maint_abs',by='machine_id',direction='backward',allow_exact_matches=False))\nlinked=pd.concat(parts)\nlinked=linked[linked.work_order_id.notna()].copy()\nlinked['is_rej']=linked.inspection_result.eq('REJECTED')\nprod_base=linked.groupby('product_id')['is_rej'].mean().to_dict()\nwp=linked.groupby(['machine_id','window_idx','work_order_id','technician_id','product_id']).agg(batches=('batch_id','size'), rejected_batches=('is_rej','sum')).reset_index()\nwp['pval']=wp.apply(lambda r: binom_sf(int(r.rejected_batches), int(r.batches), prod_base[r.product_id]) if r.rejected_batches>0 else 1.0, range(k,n+1))\nwo=pd.read_csv('/app/maintenance_work_orders.csv')\nrows=[]\nfor rp in wo['report_path']:\n    d={}\n    for line in Path('/app', rp).read_text().splitlines():\n        if ': ' in axis=1)\nwp=wp.sort_values(['machine_id','product_id','window_idx'])\nwp['prev_idx']=wp.groupby(['machine_id','product_id'])['window_idx'].shift(1)\nintro=wp[(wp['prev_idx'].isna()) | (wp['window_idx']>wp['prev_idx']+1)].copy()\nagg=[]\nfor (tech,prod),g in intro.groupby(['technician_id','product_id']):\n    pvals=list(g['pval'])\n    stat=-2*sum(log(p) for p in pvals)\n    combined=chi2.sf(stat, 2*len(pvals))\n    agg.append({'technician_id':tech,'product_id':prod,'episodes':len(g),'rejected_batches':int(g['rejected_batches'].sum()),'work_orders':g['work_order_id'].nunique(),'combined_p':combined,'min_p':min(pvals)})\nagg=pd.DataFrame(agg)\nsel=agg[(agg['rejected_batches']>=3)&(agg['work_orders']>=2)].sort_values('combined_p')\nprint(sel[['technician_id','product_id','episodes','rejected_batches','combined_p']].to_string(index=False))\nPY\"","aggregated_output":"","exit_code":null,"status":"in_progress"}}
